| <span data-ttu-id="9a07b-776">Ввод</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a07b-776">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="9a07b-777">Значение</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a07b-777">Value</span></span> |
